## enough

I've only got three pounds - not enough for a taxi. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f2b69c01b144cc1f.jpg)


She isn't going to take a taxi. 

She hasn't got enough money. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/86341d7a94a980e1.jpg)


He can't reach the shelf.  
He isn't tall enough. 

## enough + 名词 (enough money / enough people 等):

□ 'Is there enough milk in your coffee?' 'Yes, thank you.' 

□ We wanted to play football, but we didn't have enough players. 

□ Why don't you buy a car? You've got enough money. (而不用 money enough)

## enough 后也可不带名词：

□ I've got some money, but not enough to buy a car. 

(= I need more money to buy a car) 

□ 'Would you like some more to eat?' 'No, thanks. I've had enough.' 

□ You're always at home. You don't go out enough. 

形容词 + enough (good enough / tall enough 等):

□ 'Shall we sit outside?' 'No, it isn't warm enough.' (而不用 enough warm)

□ Can you hear the radio? Is it loud enough for you? 

□ Don't buy that coat. It's nice, but it isn't long enough. (= it's too short) 

## 记住：

enough + 名词 形容词 + enough

enough money 

tall enough 

enough time 

good enough 

enough people 

## 可以用：

enough for somebody/something 

□ This pullover isn't big enough for me. 

enough to do something 

□ I haven't got enough money for a new car. 

□ I haven't got enough money to buy a new car. (而不用 for buy)

enough for somebody/something to do something 

□ Is your English good enough to have a conversation? (而不用 for have)

□ There aren't enough chairs for everybody to sit down.

big eat loud milk old practise space time tired

1 We haven't got enough money to buy a new car. (money/buy)  
2 This knife isn't tomatoes. (sharp/cut)  
3 The water wasn't swimming. (warm/go)  
4 Have we got sandwiches? (bread/make)  
5 We played well, but not the game. (well/win)  
6 I don't have newspapers. (time/read)

## 92.2 用 too / too much / too many 或 enough 填空。

1 You're always at home. You don't go out enough. 

2 I don't like the weather here. There's too much rain. 

3 I can't wait for them. I haven't got ____ time. 

4 There was nowhere to sit on the beach. There were ____ people. 

5 You're always tired. I think you work .... hard. 

6 'Did you have to eat?' 'Yes, thank you.' 

7 You drink ____ coffee. It's not good for you. 

8 You don't eat ____ vegetables. You should eat more. 

9 I don't like the weather here. It's ____ cold. 

10 Our team didn't play well. We made .... mistakes. 

11 'Would you like some milk in your tea?' 'Yes, but not . 

## 92.3 用 too 或 enough 与括号中的词语完成句子。

1 I couldn't work. I was too tired. (tired) 

2 Can you turn the radio up, please? It isn't loud enough (loud) 

3 I don't want to walk home. It's ____. (far) 

4 Don't buy anything in that shop. It .... (expensive) 

5 You can't put all your things in this bag. It ____. (big) 

6 I couldn't do the exercise. It ____. (difficult) 

7 Your work needs to be better. It . (good) 

8 I can't talk to you now. I ____. (busy) 

9 I thought the film was boring. It .... (long) 

## 92.4 用 too + 形容词 + to ... 结构完成句子。

1 (I'm not going out / cold) It's too cold to go out 

2 (I'm not going to bed / early) It's 

3 (they're not getting married / young) They're 

4 (nobody goes out at night / dangerous)
It's ____ 

5 (don't phone Sue now / late)
It's ____ 

6 (I didn't say anything / surprised)
I was ____

## He speaks English very well. (词序 1)

谓语动词 + 宾语

动词 (reads) 与宾语 (a newspaper) 常连用。
通常说：

□ Sue reads a newspaper every day.
(而不用 Sue reads every day a newspaper)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e249203f36aa558b.jpg)


SUE (主语) A NEWSPAPER (宾语)

<table><tr><td>He speaks</td><td>English very well. (而不用 He speaks very well English)</td></tr><tr><td>I like</td><td>Italian food very much. (而不用 I like very much ...)</td></tr><tr><td>Did you watch</td><td>television all evening? (而不用 Did you watch all evening ...)</td></tr><tr><td>Paul often wears</td><td>a black hat. (而不用 Paul wears often ...)</td></tr><tr><td>We invited</td><td>a lot of people to the party.</td></tr><tr><td>I opened</td><td>the door slowly.</td></tr><tr><td>Why do you always make</td><td>the same mistake?</td></tr><tr><td>I&#x27;m going to borrow</td><td>some money from the bank.</td></tr></table>

## 地点 + 时间

地点状语 (where?) 常置于时间状语 (when?) 之前。通常说：

□ We went to a party last night. (而不用 We went last night to a party)

<table><tr><td></td><td>地点(where?)</td><td>+</td><td>时间(when? how long? how often?)</td></tr><tr><td>Lisa walks</td><td>to work</td><td>every day.</td><td>(而不用 ... every day to work)</td></tr><tr><td>Will you be</td><td>at home</td><td>this evening?</td><td>(而不用 ... this evening at home)</td></tr><tr><td>I usually go</td><td>to bed</td><td>early.</td><td>(而不用 ... early to bed)</td></tr><tr><td>We arrived</td><td>at the airport</td><td>at 7 o&#x27;clock.</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>They&#x27;ve lived</td><td>in the same house</td><td>for 20 years.</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>Joe&#x27;s father has been</td><td>in hospital</td><td>since June.</td><td></td></tr></table>

10 (did you buy / in England / that jacket?)
11 (every day / do / the same thing / we)
12 (football / don't like / very much / I)

## A 下列词语 (always/never 等) 常与动词连用，位于句子中间：

<table><tr><td>always</td><td>often</td><td>ever</td><td>rarely</td><td>also</td><td>already</td><td>all</td></tr><tr><td>usually</td><td>sometimes</td><td>never</td><td>seldom</td><td>just</td><td>still</td><td>both</td></tr></table>

□ My brother never speaks to me. 

□ She's always late. 

□ Do you often go to restaurants? 

□ I sometimes eat too much. (或 Sometimes I eat too much.)

□ 'Don't forget to phone Laura.' 'I've already phoned her.' 

□ I've got three sisters. They're all married. 

## always/never 等用于动词之前：

动词

<table><tr><td>always often never等</td><td>go play have等</td></tr></table>

□ I always drink coffee in the morning. 

(而不用 I drink always coffee)

□ Helen often goes to London.
(而不用 Helen goes often)

□ You sometimes look unhappy. 

□ They usually have dinner at 7 o'clock. 

□ We rarely (或 seldom) watch television.

☐ Richard is a good footballer. He also plays tennis and volleyball.
(而不用 He plays also tennis)

□ I've got three sisters. They all live in London. 

## 但 always/never 等用于 am/is/are/was/were 之后：

□ I am always tired. (而不用 I always am tired)

always □ They are never at home during the day. 

often □ It is usually very cold here in winter. 

never □ When I was a child, I was often late for school. 

□ 'Where's Laura?' 'She's still in bed.' 

□ I've got two brothers. They're both doctors. 

## always/never 等位于两个动词 (have ... been / can ... find 等) 之间：

动词1 动词2

<table><tr><td>willcando等</td><td rowspan="2">alwaysoftennever等</td><td>gofindremember等</td></tr><tr><td>havehas</td><td>gonebeen等</td></tr></table>

□ I will always remember you. 

□ It doesn't often rain here. 

□ Do you usually go to work by car? 

□ I can never find my keys. 

□ Have you ever been to Egypt? 

□ A: Where's Laura? 

B: She's just gone out. (She's = She has) 

□ My friends have all gone to the cinema.

## 94.2 用括号中的词语改写下列句子。

1 My brother speaks to me. (never) My brother never speaks to me. 

2 Susan is polite. (always) Susan. 

3 I finish work at 5 o'clock. (usually) I 

4 Sarah has started a new job. (just) Sarah 

5 I go to bed before midnight. (rarely) 

6 The bus isn't late. (usually) 

7 I don't eat fish. (often) 

8 I will forget what you said. (never) 

9 Have you lost your passport? (ever) 

10 Do you work in the same place? (still) 

11 They stay in the same hotel. (always) 

12 Jane doesn't work on Saturdays. (usually) 

13 Is Tina here? (already) 

14 What do you have for breakfast? (usually) 

15 I can remember his name. (never)

Yes, and I also play tennis.

Yes, and I 

Yes, and 

4 Have you been to England? (Ireland) 

Yes, 

5 Did you buy any clothes? (some books)

## still yet already

## an hour ago

## now

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/4d0e91f1924cd5b2.jpg)



It is still raining now.


## still 表示 “依旧，同往常一样”：

□ I had a lot to eat, but I'm still hungry. (= I was hungry before, and I'm hungry now) 

□ 'Did you sell your car?' 'No, I've still got it.' 

□ 'Do you still live in Barcelona?' 'No, I live in Madrid now.' 

## yet

## 20 minutes ago

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/125695b121797b98.jpg)



Twenty minutes ago they were waiting for Bill.


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/023bfdc5f9e8136d.jpg)



They are still waiting for Bill. Bill hasn't come yet.


## yet 表示 “直到现在”

yet 用于否定句 (He hasn't come yet.) 与疑问句 (Has he come yet?) 中，常位于句末：

□ A: Where's Emma? 

B: She isn't here yet. (= she will be here, but until now she hasn't come) 

□ A: What are you doing this evening? 

B: I don't know yet. (= I will know later, but I don't know at the moment) 

□ A: Are you ready to go yet? 

B: Not yet. In a minute. (= I will be ready, but I'm not ready at the moment) 

□ A: Have you finished with the newspaper yet? 

B: No, I'm still reading it. 

请比较 yet 与 still:

□ She hasn't gone yet. = She's still here. (而不用 she is yet here)

□ I haven't finished eating yet. = I'm still eating. 

## already 表示 “已经，比预料中的早”

□ 'What time is Joe coming?' 'He's already here.' (= earlier than we expected) 

□ 'I'm going to tell you what happened.' 'That's not necessary. I already know.' 

□ Sarah isn't coming to the cinema with us. She has already seen the film.

## 95.3 用 yet 提问。

1 You and Sue are going out together. You are waiting for her to get ready. Perhaps she is ready now. You ask her: Are you ready yet? 

2 You are waiting for Helen to arrive. She wasn't here ten minutes ago. Perhaps she is here now. You ask somebody: ____ Helen ____ 

3 Anna did an exam and is waiting for the results. Perhaps she has her results now. You ask her: ____ you ____ 

4 A few days ago you spoke to Tom. He wasn't sure where to go on holiday. Perhaps he has decided now.
You ask him: ____

## 96.3 用 Can you give me ... ? / Can you pass me ... ? 等句式提问。

1 (you want the salt) (pass) Can you pass me the salt? 

2 (you need an umbrella) (lend) Can you 

3 (you want my address) (give) Can 

4 (you need twenty pounds) (lend) 

5 (you want some information) (send) 

6 (you want to see the letter) (show) 

7 (you want some stamps) (get) 

## 96.4 从画线部分中选择正确的表达方式。

1 I gave to Sarah the keys. / I gave Sarah the keys. (I gave Sarah the keys is right) 

2 I'll lend to you some money if you want. / I'll lend you some money if you want. 

3 Did you send the letter me? / Did you send the letter to me? 

4 I want to buy for you a present. / I want to buy you a present. 

5 Can you pass to me the sugar, please? / Can you pass me the sugar, please? 

6 This is Lisa's bag. Can you give it to her? / Can you give her it? 

7 I showed to the policeman my identity card. / I showed the policeman my identity card. 

and but or so because 

这些连词用来连接两个句子，从而将两个短句并为一个长句：

A句

The car stopped. 

The driver got out. 

B句

The car stopped and the driver got out. 

## and/but/or

<table><tr><td>A句</td><td>B句</td></tr><tr><td>We stayed at home</td><td>and (we)★ watched television.</td></tr><tr><td>My sister is married</td><td>and (she)★ lives in London.</td></tr><tr><td>He doesn&#x27;t like her,</td><td>and she doesn&#x27;t like him.</td></tr><tr><td>I bought a newspaper,</td><td>but I didn&#x27;t read it.</td></tr><tr><td>It&#x27;s a nice house,</td><td>but it hasn&#x27;t got a garden.</td></tr><tr><td>Do you want to go out,</td><td>or are you too tired?</td></tr></table>

★ 不必重复 we 与 she

当多个短句并列时，用逗号(,)连接前几项，并用 and 连接最后两项：

□ I got home, had something to eat, sat down in an armchair and fell asleep. 

□ Karen is at work, Sue has gone shopping and Chris is playing football. 

so（表结果）

<table><tr><td>A句</td><td>B句</td></tr><tr><td>It was very hot,so</td><td>I opened the window.</td></tr><tr><td>Joe does a lot of sport,so</td><td>he&#x27;s very fit.</td></tr><tr><td>They don&#x27;t like travelling,so</td><td>they haven&#x27;t been to many places.</td></tr></table>

## because (表原因)

<table><tr><td colspan="2">A句</td><td>B句</td></tr><tr><td>I opened the window</td><td>because</td><td>it was very hot.</td></tr><tr><td>Joe can&#x27;t come to the party</td><td>because</td><td>he&#x27;s going away.</td></tr><tr><td>Lisa is hungry</td><td>because</td><td>she didn&#x27;t have breakfast.</td></tr></table>

## because 也常用于句首：

□ Because it was very hot, I opened the window. 

下列例句中有不止一个连词：

☐ It was late and I was tired, so I went to bed. 

□ I always enjoy visiting London, but I wouldn't like to live there because it's too big.

## when ...

□ When I went out, it was raining. 或 It was raining when I went out.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/650a5024800295ad.jpg)


Before you cross the road, always look both ways. 

## when I am ... / when I go ... 等

Lisa will be in Mexico when Sarah is in New York. 

I'll be in Mexico when you're here. 

□ When I get home this evening, I'm going to have a shower. 

□ I can't talk to you now. I'll talk to you later when I have more time. 

□ Please close the window before you go out. (而不用 before you will go)

☐ Rachel is going to stay in our flat while we are away. (而不用 while we will be)

□ I'll wait here until you come back. (而不用 until you will come back)

## if we go ...

## if you see ... 等

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/52bb6cc473f567eb.jpg)


## if 用于句首或句中：

## if 用于句首

If we go by bus, it will be cheaper. 

If you don't hurry, you'll miss the train. 

If you're hungry, have something to eat. 

If the phone rings, can you answer it, please? 

## if 用于句中

<table><tr><td>It will be cheaper</td><td>if we go by bus.</td></tr><tr><td>You&#x27;ll miss the train</td><td>if you don&#x27;t hurry.</td></tr><tr><td>I&#x27;m going to the concert</td><td>if I can get a ticket.</td></tr><tr><td>Is it OK</td><td>if I use your phone?</td></tr></table>

## 在对话中，常将 if 部分单独使用：

□ 'Are you going to the concert?' 'Yes, if I can get a ticket.' 

## If you see Ann tomorrow ... 等

if 之后常用一般现在时（而不用 will），可说 if you see ...（而不用 if you will see）：

□ If you see Ann tomorrow, can you ask her to call me? 

□ If I'm late this evening, don't wait for me. (而不用 If I will be)

□ What shall we do if it rains? (而不用 if it will rain)

□ If I don't feel well tomorrow, I'll stay at home. 

## if 与 when 比较

if I go out 表示 “如果我要出去”（不确定）:

□ A: Are you going out later? 

□ B: Maybe. If I go out, I'll close the windows. 

## when I go out 表示 “当我出去时”（肯定）：

□ A: Are you going out later? 

□ B: Yes, I am. When I go out, I'll close the windows. 

## 请比较 when 与 if:

□ When I get home this evening, I'm going to have a shower. 

□ If I'm late this evening, don't wait for me. (而不用 When I'm late)

□ We're going to play tennis if it doesn't rain. (而不用 when it doesn't rain)

## 99.1 从下列方框中各选择一个表达，并以 if 开头造句。

If + 

you don't hurry
you pass the exam
you fail the exam
you don't want this magazine
you want those pictures
you're busy now
you're hungry
you need money 

1 If you don't hurry, you'll be late. 

2 If you pass. 

3 If 

we can have lunch now
you can have them
I can lend you some
you'll get a certificate
you'll be late
I'll throw it away
we can talk later
you can do it again 

## 99.2 从画线部分中选择正确的表达形式。

1 If I'm / I'll be late this evening, don't wait for me. (I'm is right)
2 Will you call me if I give / I'll give you my phone number?
3 If there is /will be a fire, the alarm will ring.
4 If I don't see you tomorrow morning, I call / I'll call you in the evening.
5 I'm / I'll be surprised if Martin and Jane get / will get married.
6 Do you go / Will you go to the party if they invite / they'll invite you? 

## 99.3 根据你自己的想法完成下列句子。

1 I'm going to the concert if I can get a ticket.

## 99.4 用 if 或 when 填空。

1 If I'm late this evening, don't wait for me. 

2 I'm going to do some shopping now. I come back, we can have lunch. 

3 I'm thinking of going to see Tim. I go, will you come with me? 

4 you don't want to go out tonight, we can stay at home. 

5 Is it OK I close the window? 

6 John is still at school. ____ he leaves school, he wants to go to college. 

7 Shall we have a picnic tomorrow ____ the weather is good? 

8 We're going to Madrid next week. We haven't got anywhere to stay – we hope to find a hotel ____ we get there. I don't know what we'll do ____ we don't find a room. 

Dan likes fast cars, but he doesn't have one. He doesn't have enough money. 

If he had the money, he would buy a fast car. 

had 常表示过去，但在此句中不是这样。

句中的 If he had the money 表示 “假设他现在有钱的话”（但事实上他没有）。

If I had the money ... 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/88a8fedc700965a6.jpg)


<table><tr><td>If</td><td>Iyouitthey等</td><td>had / knew / lived / went (等) ..., didn&#x27;t have / didn&#x27;t know (等) ..., were ..., could ...,</td><td>Iyouitthey等</td><td>would(n&#x27;t)could(n&#x27;t)</td><td>buy ...be ...have ...go ...等</td></tr></table>

## 可以说：

□ If he had the money, he would buy a car. 

或 He would buy a car if he had the money.

I'd / she'd / they'd 等 = I would / she would / they would 等:

□ I don't know the answer. If I knew the answer, I'd tell you. 

□ It's raining, so we're not going out. We'd get wet if we went out. 

□ Jane lives in a city. She likes cities. She wouldn't be happy if she lived in the country 

□ If you didn't have a job, what would you do? (但事实上你有工作)

□ I'm sorry I can't help you. I'd help you if I could. (但事实上我不行)

□ If we had a car, we could travel more. (但事实上我们没有车，所以不能经常旅游)

## if (I) was/were

可以说 if I/he/she/it was 或 if I/he/she/it were:

□ It's not a very nice place. I wouldn't go there if I were you. (或 ... if I was you)

□ It would be nice if the weather was better.
(或 ... if the weather were better)

I wouldn't go out if I were you. 

□ What would Tom do if he were here?
(或 ... if he was here)

## 请比较：

if I have / if it is 等

□ I must go and see Helen. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/936ff60c57cce423.jpg)


If I have time, I will go today. 

(= maybe I'll have time, so maybe I'll go) 

□ I like that jacket. 

I'll buy it if it isn't too expensive. 

(= maybe it will not be too expensive) 

□ I'll help you if I can. (= maybe I can help) 

if I had / if it was 等

□ I must go and see Helen. 

If I had time, I would go today. 

(= I don't have time today, so I will not go) 

□ I like that jacket, but it's very expensive. 

I'd buy it if it wasn't so expensive. 

(= it is expensive, so I'm not going to buy it) 

□ I'd help you if I could, but I can't. 

## 100.1 完成下列句子。

<table><tr><td>1 I don&#x27;t know the answer. If I knew the answer, I&#x27;d tell you.</td></tr><tr><td>2 I have a car. I couldn&#x27;t travel very much if I didn&#x27;t have a car.</td></tr><tr><td>3 I don&#x27;t want to go out. If I to go out, I&#x27;d go.</td></tr><tr><td>4 We haven&#x27;t got a key. If we a key, we could get into the house.</td></tr><tr><td>5 I&#x27;m not hungry. I would have something to eat if I hungry.</td></tr><tr><td>6 Sue enjoys her work. She wouldn&#x27;t do it if she it.</td></tr><tr><td>7 He can&#x27;t speak any foreign languages. If he speak a foreign language, perhaps he would get a better job.</td></tr><tr><td>8 You don&#x27;t try hard enough. If you harder, you would have more success.</td></tr><tr><td>9 I have a lot to do today. If so much to do, we could go out.</td></tr></table>

100.2 用动词的适当形式填空。
1 If ____ the money, he would buy a fast car. (he/have)
2 Jane likes living in a city. She wouldn't be ____ happy if she lived in the country. (she/not/be)
3 If I wanted to learn Italian, ____ to Italy. (I/go)
4 I haven't told Helen what happened. She'd be angry if ____. (she/know)
5 If ____ a map, I could show you where I live. (we/have)
6 What would you do if ____ a lot of money? (you/win)
7 It's not a very good hotel. ____ there if I were you. (I/not/stay)
8 If ____ nearer London, we would go there more often. (we/live)
9 It's a pity you have to go now. ____ nice if you had more time. (it/be)
10 I'm not going to take the job. I'd take it if ____ better.
(the salary/be)
11 I don't know anything about cars. If the car broke down, ____ what to do. (I/not/know)
12 If you could change one thing in the world, what ____? (you/change)

<table><tr><td>we (have) a bigger house</td><td>it (be) a bit cheaper</td><td>I (watch) it</td></tr><tr><td>we (buy) a bigger house</td><td>every day (be) the same</td><td>I (be) bored</td></tr><tr><td>we (have) some pictures on the wall</td><td>the air (be) cleaner</td><td></td></tr></table>

1 I'd buy that jacket if it was a bit cheaper
2 If there was a good film on TV tonight, ...
3 This room would be nicer if ...
4 If there wasn't so much traffic, ...
5 Life would be boring if ...

7 We could invite all our friends to stay if ...
8 If we had more money, ... 

## 100.4 根据你自己的想法完成句子。

## a person who ... (定语从句 1)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/7bbc5fcd3d0c40c7.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/20839ffd0453ed3e.jpg)


I met a woman. She can speak six languages.
—— 两句

she → who 

I met a woman who can speak six languages. 

Jack was wearing a hat. It was too big for him.
—— 两句 ———

it → that 或 which

Jack was wearing a hat that was too big for him.
或

Jack was wearing a hat which was too big for him. 

who 用于指人（而非物）:

<table><tr><td>A thief is a personDo you know anybodyThe manThe people</td><td>who steals things.who can play the piano?who phonedwho work in the office</td><td>didn&#x27;t give his name.are very friendly.</td></tr></table>

## that 用于指物或指人均可：

<table><tr><td>An aeroplane is a machineEmma lives in a houseThe people</td><td>that flies.that is 400 years old.that work in the office</td><td>are very friendly.</td></tr></table>

that 可用于指人，但 who 更常见些。

which 用于指物（而非人）:

<table><tr><td>An aeroplane is a machineEmma lives in a house</td><td>which flies. (而不用 a machine who ...)which is 400 years old.</td></tr></table>

which 不用于指人:
□ Do you remember the woman who was playing the piano at the party?
(而不用 the woman which ...)

101.1 从方框中选择词语，并用 A ... is a person who ... 句式造句。遇到生词可以查词典。

<table><tr><td>a thief</td><td>a dentist</td></tr><tr><td>a butcher</td><td>a fool</td></tr><tr><td>a musician</td><td>a genius</td></tr><tr><td>a patient</td><td>a liar</td></tr></table>

doesn't tell the truth takes care of your teeth is very intelligent plays a musical instrument is ill in hospital
steals things
does stupid things
sells meat 

1 A thief is a person who steals things. 

2 A butcher is a person. 

3 A musician. 

## 101.2 将括号中的两个句子并为一句。

1 (A man phoned. He didn't give his name.) The man who phoned didn't give his name. 

2 (A woman opened the door. She was wearing a yellow dress.) The woman 

3 (Some students took the exam. Most of them passed.) Most of the students 

4 (A policeman stopped our car. He wasn't very friendly.) The 

## 101.3 用 who 或 which 填空。

1 I met a woman .... who.... can speak six languages.
2 What's the name of the man .... has just started work in your office?
3 What's the name of the river .... flows through the town?
4 Where is the picture .... was hanging on the wall?
5 Do you know anybody .... wants to buy a car?
6 You always ask questions .... are difficult to answer.
7 I have a friend .... is very good at repairing cars.
8 I think everybody .... went to the party enjoyed it very much.
9 Why does he always wear clothes .... are too small for him? 

## 101.4 判断下列句子的对错。如有错误，请改正。

1 A thief is a person which steals things.  
2 An aeroplane is a machine that flies.  
3 A coffee maker is a machine who makes coffee.  
4 Have you seen the money that was on the table;  
5 I don't like people which never stop talking.  
6 I know somebody that can help you.  
7 I know somebody who works in that shop.  
8 Correct the sentences who are wrong.  
9 My neighbour bought a car who cost £40,000. 

# the people we met the hotel you stayed at (定语从句 2)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/70053b012644963e.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a3c34ddfdc4af740.jpg)


The man is carrying a bag.
It's very heavy. } 两句

The bag (that) he is carrying is very heavy.
一句

Kate won some money.
What is she going to do with it?} 两句

What is Kate going to do with the money (that) she won? 一句

可以说：

☐ The bag that he is carrying ... 或 The bag he is carrying ... (用不用 that 均可)

□ ... the money that Kate won? 或 ... the money Kate won?

指代宾语时，that/who/which 可省略：

<table><tr><td>主语</td><td>谓语动词</td><td>宾语</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>The man</td><td>was carrying</td><td>a bag</td><td>→ the bag (that) the man was carrying</td></tr><tr><td>Kate</td><td>won</td><td>some money</td><td>→ the money (that) Kate won</td></tr><tr><td>You</td><td>wanted</td><td>some books</td><td>→ the books (that) you wanted</td></tr><tr><td>We</td><td>met</td><td>some people</td><td>→ the people (who) we met</td></tr></table>

□ Did you find the books you wanted? (或 ... the books that you wanted?)

☐ The people we met were very friendly. (或 The people who we met ...)

□ Everything I said was true. (或 Everything that I said ...)

注意：

☐ The film we saw was very good. (而不用 The film we saw it was ...)

有时谓语动词之后跟介词 (to/in/at 等):

<table><tr><td>Eve is talking to a man.</td><td>→</td><td>Do you know the man Eve is talking to?</td></tr><tr><td>We stayed at a hotel.</td><td>→</td><td>The hotel we stayed at was near the station.</td></tr><tr><td>I told you about some books.</td><td>→</td><td>These are the books I told you about.</td></tr></table>

注意：

... the books I told you about. (而不用 the books I told you about them)

可以说 (a place) where ...:

☐ The hotel where we stayed was near the station. (= The hotel we stayed at ...) 

指代主语时，who/that/which 不能省略（参见 Unit 101）：

□ I met a woman who can speak six languages. (who 为主语)

□ Jack was wearing a hat that was too big for him. (that 为主语)

a person who ..., a thing that/which ... (定语从句1) → Unit 101

## 102.1 将括号中的两个句子并为一句。

1 (Helen took some photographs. Have you seen them?) Have you seen the photographs Helen took? 

2 (You gave me a pen. I've lost it.) I've lost the ____ 

3 (Sue is wearing a jacket. I like it.) I like the ____ 

4 (I gave you some flowers. Where are they?)
Where are the ____ 

5 (He told us a story. I didn't believe it.) 

6 (You bought some oranges. How much were they?)
How 

## 102.2 将括号中的两个句子并为一句。

1 (I was carrying a bag. It was very heavy.) The bag I was carrying was very heavy. 

2 (You cooked a meal. It was excellent.) The ____ 

3 (I'm wearing shoes. They aren't very comfortable.) The shoes ____ 

4 (We invited some people to dinner. They didn't come.) The ____ 

## 102.3 根据所给信息完成句子。

1 Your friend stayed at a hotel. You ask: What's the name of ____ the hotel you stayed at ____ 

2 Your friend was talking to some people. You ask: Who are the people ____ 

3 Your friend was looking for some keys. You ask: Did you find the ____ 

4 Your friend is going to a party. You ask: Where is the ____ 

5 Your friend was talking about a film. You ask: What's the name of ____ 

6 Your friend is listening to some music. You ask: What's that ____ 

7 Your friend was waiting for a letter. You ask: Did you get ____ 

## 102.4 根据所给信息，用 where 完成问题。

1 John stayed at a hotel. You ask him:
Did you like ____ the hotel where you stayed ____ 

2 Sue had dinner in a restaurant. You ask her: What's the name of the restaurant ____ 

3 Sarah lives in a village. You ask her: How big is the ____ 

4 Richard works in a factory. You ask him: Where exactly is ____ 

at 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/aaf37e1b7b4ad3d9.jpg)


at 

8 o'clock 

10.30 

midnight 等

on 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/6204201f221f559c.jpg)


Sunday(s) / Monday(s) 等

on 

25 April / 6 June 等

New Year's Day 等

in 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/dee40f458206ee0b.jpg)


April/June 等

2003/1968 等

summer/spring 等

□ I start work at 8 o'clock. 

□ The shops close at 5.30. 

□ Bye! I'll see you on Friday. 

□ What do you usually do on Sundays? 

□ The concert is on 22 November. 

□ I'm going on holiday in October. 

□ Emma was born in 1983. 

□ The park is beautiful in spring. 

## 通常说：

at the weekend 

at night 

□ Are you going away at the weekend? 

at Christmas / at Easter 

□ I can't sleep at night. 

at the end of ... 

□ Where will you be at Christmas? (或 on Christmas Day)

at the moment 

□ I'm going on holiday at the end of October. 

□ Are you busy at the moment? 

## in the morning / in the afternoon / in the evening

□ I always feel good in the morning. 

但用

□ Do you often go out in the evening? 

## on Monday morning / on Tuesday afternoon / on Friday evening / on Saturday night 等：

□ I'm meeting Joanne on Monday morning. 

□ Are you doing anything on Saturday night? 

## at/on/in 不用于下列短语之前：

this ... (this morning / this week 等)

last ... (last August / last week 等)

next ... (next Monday / next week 等)

every ... (every day / every week 等)

□ Are you going out this evening? 

□ We go on holiday every summer.
Last summer we went to Canada. 

□ I'm leaving next Monday.
(而不用 on next Monday)

## in five minutes / in a few days / in six weeks / in two years 等

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d05e17935b83cd7c.jpg)



now



in five minutes


□ Hurry! The train leaves in five minutes. 

(= it leaves five minutes from now) 

□ Bye! I'll see you in a few days. 

(= a few days from now) 

<table><tr><td>1</td><td>on</td><td>6 June</td><td>7</td><td>24 September</td><td>13</td><td>Friday morning</td></tr><tr><td>2</td><td>in</td><td>the evening</td><td>8</td><td>Thursday</td><td>14</td><td>Saturday night</td></tr><tr><td>3</td><td></td><td>half past two</td><td>9</td><td>11.45</td><td>15</td><td>night</td></tr><tr><td>4</td><td></td><td>Wednesday</td><td>10</td><td>Christmas Day</td><td>16</td><td>the end of the day</td></tr><tr><td>5</td><td></td><td>1997</td><td>11</td><td>Christmas</td><td>17</td><td>the weekend</td></tr><tr><td>6</td><td></td><td>September</td><td>12</td><td>the morning</td><td>18</td><td>winter</td></tr></table>

## Exercises

## 103.1 用 at/on/in 填空。

## 103.2 用 at/on/in 填空。

1 Bye! See you on Friday. 11 I often go away the weekend. 

2 Where were you 28 February? 12 I'm starting my new job 3 July. 

3 I got up 8 o'clock this morning. 13 We often go to the beach summer. 

4 I like getting up early .... the morning. 14 George isn't here .... the moment. 

5 My sister got married .... May. 15 Jane's birthday is .... December. 

6 Diane and I first met 1991. 16 Do you work Saturdays? 

7 Did you go out ____ Tuesday? 17 The company started ____ 1989. 

8 Did you go out ____ Tuesday evening? 18 I like to look at the stars ____ night. 

9 Do you often go out .... the evening? 19 I'll send you the money .... the end of 

10 Let's meet 7.30 tomorrow evening. 

## 103.3 根据莉萨下周的日程安排，完成下列句子。

2 She has to phone Chris 

3 She isn't doing anything special 

4 She's got a driving lesson 

5 She's going to a party 

6 She's meeting Sam 

## 103.4 用 in ... 结构造句。

1 It's 8.25 now. The train leaves at 8.30. The train leaves in five minutes. 

2 It's Monday today. I'll call you on Thursday. I'll ____ days. 

3 Today is 14 June. My exam is on 28 June. My ____ 

4 It's 3 o'clock now. Tom will be here at 3.30. Tom ____ 

## 103.5 用 at/on/in 填空，有些句子可能不需要介词。

1 I'm going on Friday. 7 What are you doing the weekend? 

2 I'm going ____ next Friday. (already complete) 8 I phone Robert ____ every Sunday. 

3 I always feel tired ____ the evening.
9 Shall we play tennis ____ next Sunday? 

4 Will you be at home .... this evening? 10 I can't go to the party .... Sunday. 

5 We went to France .... last summer. 11 I'm going out. I'll be back .... an hour. 

6 Laura was born 1990. 12 I don't often go out night. 

## from ... to ...

□ We lived in Japan from 1992 to 2001. 

□ I work from Monday to Friday. 

也可用 from ... until ... 表达：

<table><tr><td>from Monday to Friday</td></tr></table>

□ We lived in Japan from 1992 until 2001. 

周一

周五

## until + 某一截止时间

<table><tr><td>until</td><td>FridayDecember3 o&#x27;clockI come back</td></tr></table>

□ They're going away tomorrow. 

They'll be away until Friday. 

□ I went to bed early, but I wasn't tired. 

I read a book until 3 o'clock. 

until Friday 

也可用 till 代替 until:

□ Wait here until I come back. 

周五

□ Wait here till I come back. 

请比较：

□ 'How long will you be away?' 'Until Monday.' 

□ 'When are you coming back?' 'On Monday.' 

## since + 过去某一时刻（表示“从那时起到现在”）

since 用于现在完成时 (have been / have done 等) 之后:

<table><tr><td>since</td><td>Monday19982.30I arrived</td></tr></table>

□ Joe is in hospital. He has been 

in hospital since Monday. 

(= from Monday to now) 

□ Sue and Dave have been married since 1968.
(= from 1968 to now) 

since Monday 

周一

现在

☐ It has been raining since I arrived. 

请比较：

□ We lived in Japan from 1992 to 2001. 

We lived in Japan until 2001. 

□ Now we live in Canada. We came to Canada in 2001. 

We have lived in Canada since 2001. (= from 2001 until now) 

for (而不用 since) + 某一段时间 (three days / ten years 等):

□ Joe has been in hospital for three days. (而不用 since three days)

## for + 某一段时间

<table><tr><td>for</td><td>three daysten yearsfive minutesa long time</td></tr></table>

□ Gary stayed with us for three days. 

□ I'm going away for a few weeks. 

<table><tr><td colspan="3">for three days</td></tr><tr><td>周一</td><td>周二</td><td>周三</td></tr></table>

□ I'm going away for the weekend. 

□ They've been married for ten years.

1 (Alex / Canada / 1991 → 1999) Alex lived in Canada from 1991 to 1999 

2 (Alex / Canada / → 1999) Alex lived in Canada 1999. 

3 (Alex / England / 1999 →) Alex has lived in England 

4 (Karen / France / → 2003) Karen lived in ..... 

5 (Karen / Switzerland / 2003 →) Karen has lived in 

6 (Clare / a hotel / 1998–2001) Clare worked ..... 

7 (Clare / a restaurant / 2001 →) Clare has worked 

8 (Adam / a teacher / 1992–1998) Adam was a ..... 

9 (Adam / a journalist / 1998 →) Adam has been

15 (Adam / a teacher) Adam 

16 (Adam / a journalist) Adam

## before after during while

## before, during 与 after 比较:

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/fbdfe5121febad02.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/90ed4fee8a91318f.jpg)



during the film


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/276d033896ce8679.jpg)



after the film


□ Everybody feels nervous before exams. 

□ I fell asleep during the film. 

□ We were tired after our visit to the museum. 

## before, while 与 after 比较

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/1c93fb6149108185.jpg)



before we played


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/cb7a33c130afdb87.jpg)



while we were playing


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/351aaf623d5dac19.jpg)



after we played


□ Don't forget to close the window before you go out. 

□ I often fall asleep while I'm reading. 

□ They went home after they did the shopping. 

## during, while 与 for 比较

during 之后接名词 (during the film), while 之后接句子 (while I'm reading):

□ We didn't speak during the meal. 

或 We didn't speak while we were eating. (而不用 during we were eating)

for (而不用 during) 之后接某一段时间 (three days / two hours / a year 等):

□ We played tennis for two hours. (而不用 during two hours)

□ I lived in London for a year. (而不用 during a year)

before/after 之后可接动词 -ing 形式 (before going / after eating 等):

☐ I always have breakfast before going to work. (= before I go to work) 

□ After doing the shopping, they went home. (= after they did) 

注意要说 before going (而不用 before to go), after doing (而不用 after to do) 等:

Before eating the apple, I washed it carefully. (而不用 before to eat)

☐ I started work after reading the newspaper. (而不用 after to read)

过去进行时（I was -ing）→ Units 13-14 before/after/while/when → Unit 98 for → Unit 104
介词 + -ing → Unit 112

## 105.1 从下列方框中分别选择词语，完成句子。

<table><tr><td>after before</td><td>during while</td><td>+</td><td>lunch the concert the course</td><td>the end the exam the night</td><td>they went to Australia you&#x27;re waiting</td></tr></table>

1 Everybody was nervous before the exam 

2 I usually work four hours in the morning, and another three hours 

3 The film was really boring. We left 

4 Anna went to evening classes to learn German. She learnt a lot. 

5 My aunt and uncle lived in London 

6 A: Somebody broke a window ...
B: No, I was asleep all the time. 

Did you hear anything? 

7 Would you like to sit down ____? 

8 'Are you going home ……?' 'Yes, I have to get up early tomorrow.' 

## 105.2 用 during/while/for 填空。

1 We didn't speak ____ while ____ we were eating. 

2 We didn't speak ....during.... the meal. 

3 Gary called you were out. 

4 I stayed in Rome ____ five days. 

5 Sally didn't read any newspapers .... she was on holiday. 

6 The students looked very bored ____ the lesson. 

7 I fell out of bed ....I was asleep. 

8 Last night I watched TV ____ three hours. 

9 I don't usually watch TV ____ the day. 

10 Do you ever watch TV ____ you are having dinner? 

## 105.3 用动词 -ing 形式 (doing, having 等) 完成句子。

1 After doing the shopping, they went home. 

2 I felt sick after .... too much chocolate. 

3 I'm going to ask you a question. Think carefully before it. 

4 I felt awful when I got up this morning. I felt better after ____ a shower. 

5 After ____ my work, I left the office and went home. 

6 Before ____ to a foreign country, you should try and learn a little of the language. 

## 105.4 用 before / after + -ing 形式造句。

1 They did the shopping. Then they went home.
After doing the shopping, they went home. 

2 John left school. Then he worked in a bookshop for two years.
John worked ____ 

3 I read for a few minutes. Then I went to sleep. Before ____ 

4 We walked for three hours. We were very tired.
After ____ 

5 Let's have a cup of coffee. Then we'll go out. Let's ____

## Unit 107

## 107 in at on (地点2)

## A in

<table><tr><td>in bedin hospitalin the skyin the worldin a newspaper / in a bookin a photograph / in a picturein a car / in a taxiin the middle (of...)</td><td>□‘Where’s Kate?’ ‘She’s in bed.’□David’s father is ill. He’s in hospital.□I like to look at the stars in the sky at night.□What’s the largest city in the world?□I read about the accident in the newspaper.□You look sad in this photograph.□Did you come here in your car?□There’s a big tree in the middle of the garden.</td></tr></table>

## B at

at home 

at work / at school 

at university / at college 

at the station / at the airport 

at Jane's (house) / at my sister's (house) / 

at the doctor's / at the hairdresser's 等

at a concert / at a party / at a football match 等

□ Will you be at home this evening? 

□ 'Where's Kate?' 'She's at work.' 

□ Helen is studying law at university. 

□ I'll meet you at the station, OK? 

□ A: Where were you yesterday? 

B: At my sister's. 

□ I saw Tom at the doctor's. 

□ There weren't many people at the party. 

in 或 at 可用于建筑物（宾馆、餐馆等）之前：
□ We stayed at a nice hotel. 或 We stayed in a nice hotel.

## on

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/86fe2f6c908a1a32.jpg)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/2e2a375a1fbc4414.jpg)

on the way from A to B


on a bus / on a train / on a plane / on a ship 

on the ground floor / on the first floor 等

on the way (to ...) / on the way home 

□ Did you come here on the bus? 

□ The office is on the first floor.
(而不用 in the first floor)

□ I met Ann on the way to work / on the way home.

## 107.2 用 in/at/on 填空。

1 Helen is studying law at university. 

2 There was a big table ____ the middle of the room. 

3 What is the longest river ____ the world? 

4 Were there many people .... the concert last night? 

5 Will you be .... home tomorrow afternoon? 

6 Who is the man .... this photograph? Do you know him? 

7 Where are your children? Are they ____ school? 

8 Gary is coming by train. I'm going to meet him ____ the station. 

9 Charlie is .... hospital. He had an operation yesterday. 

10 How many pages are there .... this book? 

11 'Are you hungry after your journey?' 'No, I had something to eat ____ the train.' 

12 I'm sorry I'm late. My car broke down .... the way here. 

13 'Is Tom here?' 'No, he's ... his brother's.' 

14 Don't believe everything you see .... the newspaper! 

15 I walked to work, but I came home .... the bus. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/55312ad6f1ca8642.jpg)


## go/come/return/walk (等) to ...

to London 

□ We're going to London on Sunday. 

□ I want to go to Italy next year. 

□ We walked from my house to the centre of town. 

□ What time do you go to bed? 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/8fdcd9156e84c79a.jpg)


□ The bus is going to the airport. 

□ Karen didn't go to work yesterday. 

□ I went to a party last night. 

□ You must come to our house. 

## home

go/come/walk (等) home (不带 to):

□ I'm tired. I'm going home. 

(而不用 to home)

□ Did you walk home? 

## in/at (参见 Units 106-107)

## be/stay/do something (等) in ...

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/df302c74b4613114.jpg)


□ Piccadilly Circus is in London. 

□ My brother lives in Italy. 

☐ The main shops are in the centre of town. 

□ I like reading in bed. 

## be/stay/do something (等) at ...

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/80ce736949de4fbc.jpg)


□ The bus is at the airport. 

□ Sarah wasn't at work yesterday. 

□ I met a lot of people at the party. 

□ Helen stayed at her brother's house. 

be/stay/do something (等) at home:

□ I'm staying at home tonight. 

□ Dan doesn't go to an office. He works at home. 

## arrive 与 get 比较

arrive in 后接国家或城镇 (arrive in Italy / arrive in Paris 等):

□ They arrived in England last week. (而不用 arrived to England)

arrive at 后接其他地点 (arrive at the station / arrive at work 等):

□ What time did you arrive at the hotel? (而不用 arrive to the hotel)

get to 后接地点：

□ What time did you get to the hotel? 

□ What time did you get to Paris? 

get home / arrive home (不带介词):

□ I was tired when I got home. 或 I was tired when I arrived home.

## 08.1 用 to 或 in 填空。

1 I like reading in bed. 

2 We're going .... Italy next month. 

5 I was tired, so I stayed .... bed late. 

6 What time do you usually go .... bed? 

3 Sue is on holiday .... Italy at the moment. 

7 Does this bus go .... the centre? 

4 I have to go .... the bank today. 

8 Would you like to live .... another country? 

## 108.2 用 to 或 at 填空，其中有一句不需要介词。

1 Paula didn't go to work yesterday. 

2 I'm tired. I'm going .... home. (already complete) 

3 Tina is not very well. She has gone ____ the doctor. 

4 Would you like to come .... a party on Saturday? 

5 'Is Liz .... home?' 'No, she's gone .... work.' 

6 There were 20,000 people .... the football match. 

7 Why did you go .... home early last night? 

8 A boy jumped into the river and swam ____ the other side. 

9 There were a lot of people waiting .... the bus stop. 

10 We had a good meal ....a restaurant, and then we went back ....the hotel. 

## 108.3 用 to, at 或 in 填空，其中有一句不需要介词。

1 I'm not going out this afternoon. I'm staying at home. 

2 We're going .... a concert tomorrow evening. 

3 I went .... New York last year. 

4 How long did you stay .... New York? 

5 Next year we hope to go ...... Canada to visit some friends. 

6 Do you want to go .... the cinema this evening? 

7 Did you park your car ____ the station? 

8 After the accident three people were taken .... hospital. 

9 How often do you go .... the dentist? 

10 'Is Sarah here?' 'No, she's ... Helen's.' 

11 My house is .... the end of the street on the left. 

12 I went ....Maria's house, but she wasn't ....home. 

13 There were no taxis, so we had to walk .... home. 

14 'Who did you meet ____ the party?' 'I didn't go ____ the party.' 

## 108.4 用 to, at 或 in 填空，有些句子可能不需要介词。

1 What time do you usually get .... work? 4 When did you arrive .... London? 

2 What time do you usually get .... home? 5 What time does the train get .... Paris? 

3 What time did you arrive .... the party? 6 We arrived .... home very late. 

## 108.5 根据你自己的情况，用 to/in/at 完成句子。

1 At three o'clock this morning I was in bed 

3 At 11 o'clock yesterday morning I was 

4 One day I'd like to go 

5 I don't like going. 

6 At 9 o'clock yesterday evening I was 

## next to / beside / between / in front of / behind

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/2a3daa9424c4dc3a.jpg)


A is next to B. 或 A is beside B.
B is between A and C.
D is in front of B.
E is behind B.

也可以说：  
A is on the left.  
C is on the right.  
B is in the middle (of the group).

## opposite / in front of

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3d2cc57ae8116266.jpg)


A is sitting in front of B.  
A is sitting opposite C.  
C is sitting opposite A. 

## by (= next to / beside)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/93604e734a86a799.jpg)


by the window 

☐ Our house is by the sea. (= beside the sea) 

□ Who is that man standing by the window? 

□ If you feel cold, why don't you sit by the fire? 

## under

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e85bd619e193d296.jpg)


under the table 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/048381d385093a14.jpg)



under a tree


□ The cat is under the table.
□ The girl is standing under a tree.
□ I'm wearing a jacket under my coat. 

## above 与 below 比较

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f22e7800174dfa62.jpg)


A is above the line. (= higher than the line) 

B 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5944836537e0fc7d.jpg)


B is below the line. (= lower than the line) 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/17d23b7fc561802f.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/5af8f6cd2879e9dd.jpg)



The pictures are above the shelves.


The shelves are below the pictures. 

109.1 图中的人物分别在什么位置？完成下列句子。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/ded28db850c954b5.jpg)



DONNA EMMA FRANK


1 Colin is standing behind Frank. 

2 Frank is sitting .... Emma. 

3 Emma is sitting ____ Barbara. 

4 Emma is sitting ____ Donna and Frank. 

5 Donna is sitting .... Emma. 

6 Frank is sitting ....Colin. 

7 Alan is standing ____ Donna. 

8 Alan is standing .... left. 

9 Barbara is standing .... middle.

## Unit 110

## up, over, through 等

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/06135c844e315c65.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/4001cd0760b2f855.jpg)



into (in)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/dd9137037a523346.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/dd0a95bda793d02f.jpg)


□ Jane is going to France next week. 

☐ We walked from the hotel to the station. 

☐ A lot of English words come from Latin. 

□ We jumped into the water. 

□ A man came out of the house and got into a car. 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/783036a0be8001c0.jpg)



out of


□ Why are you looking out of the window?
□ I took the old batteries out of the radio. 

要说 put something in ... (而通常不用 into):
□ I put new batteries in the radio.

□ Don't put your feet on the table.
□ Please take your feet off the table.
□ I'm going to hang some pictures on the wall.
□ Be careful! Don't fall off your bicycle.
□ We got on the bus in Princes Street.

□ Be careful! Don't fall down the stairs.

□ We walked around the town.

## 110.2 看图并用介词完成句子。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e131b3d5af459d92.jpg)


1 The dog swam across the river. 6 Suddenly a car came the corner. 

2 A book fell ____ the shelf. 7 They drove ____ the village. 

3 A plane flew ____ the village. 8 They got ____ the train. 

4 A woman got ____ the car. 9 The moon travels ____ the earth.

## 110.3 填入介词 over/from/round 等。

1 I looked ____ the window and watched the people in the street. 

2 My house is very near here. It's just ____ the corner. 

3 'Where's my phone?' 'You put it .... your bag.' 

4 How far is it .... here .... the airport? 

5 We walked ____ the museum for an hour and saw a lot of interesting things. 

6 You can put your coat ____ the back of the chair. 

7 In tennis, you have to hit the ball ____ the net. 

8 Silvia took a key ____ her bag and opened the door. 

## Unit 111

## on at by with about

A 

## on

on holiday 

on television 

□ Jane isn't at work this week. She's on holiday. 

on the radio 

□ We watched the news on television. 

on the phone 

□ We listened to the news on the radio. 

on fire 

□ I spoke to Rachel on the phone last night. 

on time (准时)

☐ The house is on fire! Call the fire brigade. 

□ 'Was the train late?' 'No, it was on time.' 

## at

at (the age of) 21 / at 50 kilometres an hour / at 100 degrees 等:
□ Lisa got married at 21. (或 ... at the age of 21.)
□ A car uses more petrol at 120 kilometres an hour than at 90.
□ Water boils at 100 degrees Celsius.

## by

by car / by bus / by plane / by bike 等：
□ Do you like travelling by train?
□ Jane usually goes to work by bike.

## 但用 on foot:

□ You can't get there by car. You have to go on foot. (= you have to walk) 

a book by ... / a painting by ... / a piece of music by ... 等:

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/876fb65316008d8f.jpg)


## by bus

□ Have you read any books by Charles Dickens? 

□ Who is that painting by? Picasso? 

标题
by
作者

by 用于被动语态之后 (参见 Unit 21):

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/c200c4242f949d8f.jpg)


□ I was bitten by a dog. 

## with/without

□ Did you stay at a hotel or with friends?
□ Wait for me. Please don't go without me.
□ Do you like your coffee with or without milk?
□ I cut the paper with a pair of scissors. 

可用 a man with a beard / a woman with glasses 等结构：
□ Do you know that man with the beard?
□ I'd like to have a house with a big garden.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e9611362e4011dc0.jpg)



a man
with a beard


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/918cd16194a96268.jpg)



a woman
with glasses


## about

talk/speak/think/hear/know about ...: 

☐ Some people talk about their work all the time. 

□ I don't know much about cars. 

a book / a question / a programme / information (等) about ...

☐ There was a programme about volcanoes on TV last night. Did you see it? 

by → Units 21, 63, 109 at/on → Units 103, 106-107 介词 + -ing → Unit 112

holiday the phone the radio television time

6 She's listening to some music .... Mozart.

## 111.3 用介词 at/by/with 等完成句子。

## afraid of ..., good at ... 等 of/at/for 等（介词）+ -ing

## afraid of ... / good at ... 等（形容词 + 介词）

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/68dc68a749034b72.jpg)


angry with somebody 

angry about something 

different from ...
或 different to ...

fed up with ... 

nice/kind of somebody to ... 

be nice/kind to somebody 

sorry about (a situation) 

sorry for/about doing something 

be/feel sorry for somebody 

□ Are you afraid of dogs? 

□ Why are you angry with me? What have I done? 

□ Are you angry about last night? (= something that happened last night) 

□ Lisa is very different from (或 to) her sister.

□ I'm fed up with my job. I want to do something different. (= I've had enough of my job) 

☐ The room was full of people. 

□ Are you good at maths? 

□ I'm not interested in sport. 

□ Sue is married to a dentist. (= her husband is a dentist) 

☐ It was kind of you to help us. Thank you very much. 

□ David is very friendly. He's always very nice to me. 

□ I'm afraid I can't help you. I'm sorry about that. 

□ I'm sorry for/about not phoning you yesterday. (或 I'm sorry I didn't phone you)

□ I feel sorry for them. They are in a very difficult situation. 

## of/at/for (等) + -ing

介词 (of/at/for 等) 之后的动词用 -ing 形式:

(= he didn&#x27;t say goodbye)the shopping, they went home.</td></tr></table>

## listen to ..., look at ... 等

## look at / look for / look after

## look at ...

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/9a06e0a36022c6dd.jpg)


look for ... 

(寻找)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d07ce5a56cc2e32c.jpg)


(照顾，看管)


□ He's looking at his watch.


□ Look at these flowers! They're beautiful. 


□ Why are you looking at me like that?


□ She's lost her key. She's looking for it. 

□ I'm looking for Sarah. Have you seen her? 

□ When Emily is at work, a friend of hers looks after her children. 

□ Don't lose this book. Look after it. (= Keep it safe.) 

## C

## depend

可以说 depend on ...:

□ A: Do you like eating in restaurants? 

B: Sometimes. It depends on the restaurant. (而不用 it depends of)

it depends what/where/how（等）之后用不用 on 均可：

□ A: Do you want to come out with us? 

B: It depends where you're going. 或 It depends on where you're going.

wait $\rightarrow$ Unit 54 介词 $+$ -ing $\rightarrow$ Unit 112

## Exercises

## 113.1 看图并用介词 to/for/at 等完成句子。

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b14e3c6873550613.jpg)


1 She's looking at her watch. 4 Paul is talking Jane. 

2 He's listening ____ the radio.
5 They're looking ____ a picture. 

3 They're waiting .... a taxi. 6 Sue is looking .... Tom. 

## 113.2 用介词 to/for/about 等完成下列句子。其中有一句不需要介词。

1 Thank you very much for your help. 

2 This isn't my umbrella. It belongs ...... a friend of mine. 

3 (on the phone) Can I speak ...... Steven Davis, please? 

4 (on the phone) Thank you ____ calling. Goodbye. 

5 What happened .... Ella last night? Why didn't she come to the party? 

6 We're thinking .... going to Australia next year. 

7 We asked the waiter .... coffee, but he brought us tea. 

8 'Do you like reading books?' 'It depends .... the book.' 

9 John was talking, but nobody was listening .... what he was saying. 

10 We waited .... Karen until 2 o'clock, but she didn't come. 

11 If you want to contact me, you can write ____ me at this address. 

12 Don't forget to phone .... your mother tonight. 

13 He's alone all day. He never talks ____ anybody. 

14 'How much does it cost to stay at this hotel?' 'It depends ____ the type of room.' 

15 Catherine is thinking .... changing her job. 

## 113.3 用 at/for/after 完成下列句子。

1 I looked ____ the newspaper, but I didn't read it carefully. 

2 When you are ill, you need somebody to look .... you. 

3 Excuse me, I'm looking .... Hill Street. Can you tell me where it is? 

4 Goodbye! Have a great holiday and look .... yourself. 

5 I want to take a photograph of you. Please look ____ the camera and smile. 

6 Barry is looking ____ a job. He wants to work in a hotel. 

## 113.4 用 It depends ... 结构回答下列问题。

Do you want to go out with us?
Do you like eating in restaurants?
Do you enjoy watching TV?
Can you do something for me?
Are you going away this weekend?
Can you lend me some money? 

It depends where you're going. It depends on the restaurant. 

It depends

(= get out of bed)□ We looked up at the stars in the sky.</td><td>down↓ <img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/41067b5aef258697.jpg"/> <img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/aa9586bd375c9ab6.jpg"/>□ The picture fell down.□ Would you like to sit down?□ Lie down on the floor.</td></tr><tr><td>away / off<img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3f4be51e0a7effee.jpg"/> <img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/2f236cd2ed752249.jpg"/>□ The thief ran away. (或 ... ran off)□ Emma got into the car and drove away. (或 ... drove off)be/go away(在别处/去别处)□ Tim has gone away for a few days.</td><td>back<img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/9bc1126aa36445b5.jpg"/>□ Go away and don’t come back!□ We went out for dinner and then went back to our hotel.be back□ Tim is away. He’ll be back on Monday.</td></tr><tr><td>over<img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/de2b04b307f84c08.jpg"/> <img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/83cace52d694e34d.jpg"/> <img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0db1a609ec8fde72.jpg"/>CLIMB OVER TURNOVER□ The wall wasn’t very high, so we climbed over.□ Turn over and look at the next page.</td><td>round (或 around)<img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/bb4e8cc55a66557b.jpg"/> <img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/e5283770222e3e95.jpg"/>LOOK ROUND□ Somebody shouted my name, so I looked round (或around).□ We went for a long walk. After an hour we turned round (或around) and went back.</td></tr></table>

## Unit 115

# put your shoes on

## (短语动词 2)

有时短语动词 (put on / take off 等) 带宾语。例如：

动词 宾语

put on your coat 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/d4e545a3f8baf44a.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/3ca2c5644ccb93e1.jpg)


或 put your coat on动词 宾语
take off your shoes

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/afbedecaa0687be9.jpg)


可以说：take off your shoes或 take your shoes off

但 it/them（代词）作宾语时，总是用于 on/off 等之前：
put it on (而不用 put on it) take them off (而不用 take off them)

□ It was cold, so I put on my coat.
(或 I put my coat on)

□ Here's your coat. Put it on. 

□ Your shoes are dirty. Take them off. 

## 类似的还有：

turn on / turn off (灯、机器、龙头等):

□ It was dark, so I turned on the light.
(或 I turned the light on)

□ I don't want to watch this programme. You can turn it off. 

也可用 switch on / switch off (灯、机器等):

TURN OFF 

□ I switched on the light and switched off the television. 

pick up / put down: 

☐ Those are my keys on the floor. Can you pick them up for me? 

□ I stopped reading and put my book down. 

(或 put down my book)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f21636ec8ddcfc74.jpg)


☐ I took my new sweater back to the shop. It was too small for me. 

□ You can take my umbrella, but please bring it back. 

OFF 

□ I've got Rachel's keys. I have to give them back to her. 

□ I read the letter and then put it back in the envelope. 

bring back / take back / give back / put back: 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b5b2e64e2cbe2a0b.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/de3faa87a69417cb.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/6f4fa39c6392d1b9.jpg)

## 附录 1

## 主动语态与被动语态比较

## 1.1 现在时与过去时

<table><tr><td colspan="2">主动语态</td><td>被动语态</td></tr><tr><td>一般现在时</td><td>□ We make butter from milk.□ Somebody cleans these rooms every day.□ People never invite me to parties.□ How do they make butter?</td><td>□ Butter is made from milk.□ These rooms are cleaned every day.□ I am never invited to parties.□ How is butter made?</td></tr><tr><td>一般过去时</td><td>□ Somebody stole my car last week.□ Somebody stole my keys yesterday.□ They didn&#x27;t invite me to the party.□ When did they build these houses?</td><td>□ My car was stolen last week.□ My keys were stolen yesterday.□ I wasn&#x27;t invited to the party.□ When were these houses built?</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3"></td></tr><tr><td>现在进行时</td><td>□ They are building a new airport at the moment. (= it isn&#x27;t finished)□ They are building some new houses near the river.</td><td>□ A new airport is being built at the moment.□ Some new houses are being built near the river.</td></tr><tr><td>过去进行时</td><td>□ When I was here a few years ago,they were building a new airport. (= it wasn&#x27;t finished at that time)</td><td>□ When I was here a few years ago, a new airport was being built.</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3"></td></tr><tr><td>现在完成时</td><td>□ Look! They have painted the door.□ These shirts are clean. Somebody has washed them.□ Somebody has stolen my car.</td><td>□ Look! The door has been painted.□ These shirts are clean. They have been washed.□ My car has been stolen.</td></tr><tr><td>过去完成时</td><td>□ Tina said that somebody had stolen her car.</td><td>□ Tina said that her car had been stolen.</td></tr></table>

## 1.2 will / can / must / have to 等

<table><tr><td>主动语态</td><td>被动语态</td></tr><tr><td>□ Somebody will clean the office tomorrow.□ Somebody must clean the office.□ I think they&#x27;ll invite you to the party.□ They can&#x27;t repair my watch.□ You should wash this sweater by hand.□ They are going to build a new airport.□ Somebody has to wash these clothes.□ They had to take the injured man to hospital.</td><td>□ The office will be cleaned tomorrow.□ The office must be cleaned.□ I think you&#x27;ll be invited to the party.□ My watch can&#x27;t be repaired.□ This sweater should be washed by hand.□ A new airport is going to be built.□ These clothes have to be washed.□ The injured man had to be taken to hospital.</td></tr></table>

## 不规则动词分类表

## 过去式与过去分词形式相同：

```txt
cost → cost
cut → cut
hit → hit
hurt → hurt 
```

```txt
feel → felt
leave → left
meet → met
dream → dreamt (dremt)*
mean → meant (ment)* 
```

```txt
bring → brought (brort)*  
buy → bought (bort)*  
fight → fought (fort)*  
think → thought (thort)*  
catch → caught (kort)*  
teach → taught (tort)* 
```

```txt
find → found
have → had
hear → heard
hold → held
read → read (red)*
say → said (sed)* 
```

```txt
pay → paid
make → made 
```

过去式与过去分词形式不同：

```txt
break → broke broken  
choose → chose chosen  
speak → spoke spoken  
steal → stole stolen  
wake → woke woken 
```

```txt
blow → blew blown
grow → grew grown
know → knew known
throw → threw thrown
fly → flew flown
draw → drew drawn
show → showed shown 
```

## 附录4

## 缩略形式（he's / l'd / don't 等）

## 4.1 英语口语中常将 I am 发为一个音。缩略形式 I'm 就是用来表示这种发音的一种方式：

```txt
I am → I'm
it is → it's
they have → they've
等
□ I'm feeling tired this morning.
□ 'Do you like this jacket?' 'Yes, it's nice.'
□ 'Where are your friends?' 'They've gone home.'
```

缩略形式用撇号（）表示：

```txt
I am → I'm he is → he's you have → you've she will → she'll 
```

## 4.2 I/he/she 等后接缩略形式：

<table><tr><td rowspan="13">am → &#x27;m is → &#x27;s are → &#x27;re have → &#x27;ve has → &#x27;s had → &#x27;d will → &#x27;ll would → &#x27;d</td><td rowspan="13">I&#x27;m he&#x27;s I&#x27;ve he&#x27;s he&#x27;d he&#x27;d he&#x27;ll he&#x27;d</td><td rowspan="13">she&#x27;s</td><td rowspan="13">it&#x27;s</td><td rowspan="13">we&#x27;re we&#x27;ve</td><td rowspan="13">you&#x27;re you&#x27;ve</td><td rowspan="13">they&#x27;re they&#x27;ve</td></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr><tr></tr></table>


□ I've got some new shoes. 



□ We'll probably go out this evening. 



□ It's 10 o'clock. You're late again. 


## 's = is 或 has:

□ She's going out this evening. (she's going = she is going) 

□ She's gone out. (she's gone = she has gone) 

## 'd = would 或 had:

□ A: What would you like to eat? 

B: I'd like a salad, please. (I'd like = I would like) 

☐ I told the police that I'd lost my passport. (I'd lost = I had lost) 

## 'm/'s/'d 等不用于句尾 (参见 Unit 40):

□ 'Are you tired?' 'Yes, I am.' (而不用 Yes, I'm.)

□ She isn't tired, but he is. (而不用 he's)

## 4.3 除 I/you/he/she 等外，其他一些词语也可以后接缩略形式（尤其是 's）：

□ Who's your favourite singer? (= who is) 

□ What's the time? (= what is) 

□ There's a big tree in the garden. (= there is) 

□ My sister's working in London. (= my sister is working) 

□ Paul's gone out. (= Paul has gone out) 

□ What colour's your car? (= What colour is your car?) 

## 附录 4 缩略形式（he's / l'd / don't 等）

## 4.4 否定式的缩略形式（参见 Unit 43）：

```txt
isn't (= is not)
aren't (= are not)
wasn't (= was not)
weren't (= were not)
hasn't (= has not)
haven't (= have not)
hadn't (= had not)

don't (= do not)
doesn't (= does not)
didn't (= did not)

can't (= cannot)
couldn't (= could not)
won't (= will not)
wouldn't (= would not)
shouldn't (= should not)
mustn't (= must not) 
```

```txt
□ We went to her house, but she wasn't at home. 
```

```txt
□ 'Where's David?' 'I don't know. I haven't seen him.' 
```

```txt
□ You work all the time. You shouldn't work so hard. 
```

```txt
□ I won't be here tomorrow. (= I will not) 
```

## 4.5 's (撇号 + s) 可表示不同的意思：

(1) $s = \mathbf{i}\mathbf{s}$ 或 has (参见附录4.2)

```txt
(2) let's = let us (参见 Units 35, 53)
□ It's a lovely day. Let's go out. (= Let us go out.)
```

```txt
(3) Kate's camera = her camera
my brother's car = his car
the manager's office = his/her office 等
(参见 Unit 64)
```

## 请比较：

□ Kate's camera was very expensive. (Kate's camera = her camera) 

```txt
□ Kate's a very good photographer. (Kate's = Kate is) 
```

```txt
□ Kate's got a new camera. (Kate's got = Kate has got) 
```

```txt
名词 + s (复数) (参见 Unit 66):
bird → birds mistake → mistakes hotel → hotels
动词 + s (he/she/it -s) (参见 Unit 5):
think → thinks live → lives remember → remembers
但是:
以 -s / -sh / -ch / -x 结尾的单词 + es:
bus → buses pass → passes address → addresses
dish → dishes wash → washes finish → finishes
watch → watches teach → teaches sandwich → sandwiches
box → boxes
还有:
potato → potatoes tomato → tomatoes
do → does go → goes
-f / -fe → -ves:
shelf → shelves knife → knives 但是 roof → roofs
```

## 附录5

## 拼写

## 5.1 单词变成以 -s 或 -es 结尾 (birds/watches 等):

## 5.2 以 -y 结尾的单词变法如下 (baby → babies / study → studied 等):

```txt
-y → -ies:
study → studies (而不用 studys) family → families (而不用 familys)
story → stories city → cities baby → babies
try → tries marry → marries fly → flies
-y → -ied (参见 Unit 11):
study → studied (而不用 studied)
try → tried marry → married copy → copied
-y → -ier/-iest (参见 Units 87, 90):
easy → easier/easiest (而不用 easier/easyest)
happy → happier/happiest lucky → luckier/luckiest
heavy → heavier/heaviest funny → funnier/funniest
-y → -ily (参见 Unit 86):
easy → easily (而不用 easily)
happy → happily heavy → heavily lucky → luckily
```

```txt
以 -ay/-ey/-oy/-uy 结尾的单词则不将 y 变为 i:
holiday → holidays (而不用 holidays)
enjoy → enjoys/enjoyed    stay → stays/stayed    buy → buys    key → keys
但是:
say → said    pay → paid    (不规则动词)
```

## 附录 5

## 拼写

## 5.3 动词变成 -ing 形式：

```txt
以 -e 结尾的动词（make/write/drive 等）→ -ing:
make → making    write → writing    come → coming    dance → dancing
以 -ie 结尾的动词 → -ying:
lie → lying    die → dying    tie → tying
```

5.4 单词末尾字母双写（stop → stopped, big → bigger 等）规则如下：

```txt
元音与辅音字母有：
元音字母：a e i o u
辅音字母：b c d f g k l m n p r s t w y
```

有些单词以一个元音字母加一个辅音字母结尾，如：stop，big，get。
以辅音字母 p/g/t 等结尾的单词，双写该字母变成 pp/gg/tt 等，再加 -ing/-ed/-er/-est。
例如：

```txt
V+C
stop ST O P p → pp stopping stopped C = 元音
run R U N n → nn running
get G E T t → tt getting
swim SW I M m → mm swimming
big B I G g → gg bigger biggest
hot H O T t → tt hotter hottest
thin TH I N n → nn thinner thinnest
```

下列情况则例外：

(1) 单词以两个辅音字母结尾 (C + C):

```txt
C+C
help HE L P helping helped
work WO R K working worked
fast FA S T faster fastest 
```

(2) 单词以两个元音字母加一个辅音字母结尾 $(V + V + C)$ :

```txt
V+V+C
need N E E D needing needed
wait W A I T waiting waited
cheap CH E A P cheaper cheapest 
```

(3) 单词由两个或两个以上音节构成，且最后一部分不重读：

```txt
重音
happen HAP-pen → happening/happened (而不用 happened)
visit VIS-it → visiting/visited
remember re-MEM-ber → remembering/remembered
```

```txt
但是：
prefer pre-FER (重音在词尾) → preferring/preferred
begin be-GIN (重音在词尾) → beginning
```

```txt
(4) 单词以 -y 或 -w 结尾（词尾的 y 与 w 不发辅音）：
enjoy → enjoying/enjoyed snow → snowing/snowed few → fewer/fewest
```

# 附录 6 短语动词（take off / give up 等）

以下所列的是一些重要的短语动词（参见 Unit 114）。

on 

carry on 继续

□ Don't stop working. Carry on. (= continue working) 

□ A: Excuse me, where is the station? 

B: Carry on along this road and turn right at the lights. (= Continue along ...) 另外: go on / walk on / drive on 等 继续进行 / 行走 / 开车等

□ Don't stop here. Drive on. 

come on 赶快

□ Come on! Everybody is waiting for you. 

get on（在工作、学业、考试等中）进展□ How was your exam? How did you get on? (= how did you do?)

hold on 等一下

□ Can you hold on a minute? (= can you wait?) 

take off (飞机) 起飞

☐ The plane took off 20 minutes late, but arrived on time. 

go off（炸弹等）爆炸或（警报、闹钟等）响

□ A bomb went off and caused a lot of damage. 

□ A car alarm goes off if somebody tries to break into the car. 

## up give up 放弃

□ I know it's difficult, but don't give up. (= don't stop trying) 

grow up 长大成人

□ What does your son want to do when he grows up? 

hurry up 赶快

□ Hurry up! We haven't got much time. 

speak up 大声点说

□ I can't hear you. Can you speak up, please? 

wake up 醒来

□ I often wake up in the middle of the night. 

wash up 饭后洗餐具

□ Do you want me to wash up?
(或 ... to do the washing-up?)

## down

slow down 减速

□ You're driving too fast. Slow down! 

break down（车、机器等）出故障

□ Sue was very late because her car broke down. 

## over

fall over 失去平衡，摔倒

□ I fell over because my shoes were too big for me.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f811befcde30f5b7.jpg)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/10c2e70ec7206b22.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/f7bdd56df0ac358a.jpg)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b47180cb40e04251.jpg)

CROSS OUT 

以下所列的是一些重要的可接宾语的短语动词（参见 Unit 115）。

in/out fill in / fill out 填写（表格）
□ Can you fill in this form, please? 或
Can you fill out this form, please?

out put out 熄灭（火、香烟等）
□ The fire brigade arrived and put the fire out.
cross out 划掉（出错处、单词等）
□ If you make a mistake, cross it out.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/c35b3ef844b0601a.jpg)


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/81e78fdc83283d80.jpg)


on try on 试穿(衣服)
□ (in a shop) This is a nice jacket. Shall I try it on?

up give up 放弃（某事物）
□ Sue gave up her job when her baby was born. (= she stopped working)
□ 'Are you still learning Italian?' 'No, I gave it up.'

look up（在词典等中）查找
□ I didn't know the meaning of the word, so I looked it up in a dictionary.

turn up 调高（电视、收音机、音乐等的音量，暖气的热度等）
□ Can you turn the radio up? I can't hear it.

wake up 叫醒（某人）
□ I have to get up early tomorrow. Can you wake me up at 6.30?

down knock down 拆毁（建筑物）
□ They are going to knock down the school and build a new one.

turn down 调低（电视、收音机、音乐等的音量，暖气的热度等）
□ The music is too loud. Can you turn it down?

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/b622b778e96cdb55.jpg)


over knock over 打翻（杯子等），撞倒（某人等）
□ Be careful. Don't knock your cup over.
□ There was an accident at the end of the road. A man was knocked over by a car. (或 A man was knocked down by a car.)

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a5818c86bd34ef18.jpg)



KNOCK OVER


![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/1697d692d0341402.jpg)



KNOCK OVER 或
KNOCK DOWN


away throw away 扔掉（垃圾、不想要的东西）
□ These apples are bad. Shall I throw them away?
□ Don't throw away that picture. I want it.

THROW AWAY 

put away 存放 (某物)
□ After they finished playing, the children put their toys away.

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/0ddbadaa028416fe.jpg)


back pay back 还 (某人) 的钱
□ Thank you for lending me the money. I'll pay you back next week.

round/ show round/around 领着（某人）参观
around □ We visited a factory last week. The manager showed us round.

2 'How are your parents?' 'They're fine.' 

3 'Is Anna at home?' 'No, ____ at work.' 

4 '____ my keys?' 'On your desk.' 

5 Where is Paul from? ____ American or British? 

6 ____ very hot today. The temperature is 38 degrees. 

7 'Are you a teacher?' 'No, a student.' 

8 ' your umbrella?' 'Green.' 

9 Where's your car? ____ in the car park? 

10 '____tired?' 'No, I'm fine.' 

11 'These shoes are nice. How ……?' 'Fifty pounds.'

## 3 用括号中的词语造句。

B: They're watching TV. (they / watch / TV)

B: Where's she going? (where / she / go?) 

3 A: Where's David?
B: ____ (he / have / a shower) 

4 A: ____ ? (the children / play?) 

5 A: ____ ? (it / rain?)
B: No, not at the moment. 

6 A: Where are Sue and Steve? 

B: ____ (they / come / now) 

7 A: ____? (why / you / stand / here?)
B: ____ (I / wait / for somebody)

## 9 从画线部分中选择正确的表达形式。

1 'Are you speaking / Do you speak English?' 'Yes, a little.' (Do you speak is right) 

2 Sometimes we're going / we go away at weekends. 

3 It's a nice day today. The sun is shining / shines. 

4 (You meet Kate in the street.) Hello, Kate. Where are you going / do you go? 

5 How often are you going / do you go on holiday? 

6 Emily is a writer. She's writing / She writes books for children. 

7 I'm never reading / I never read newspapers. 

8 'Where are Michael and Jane?' 'They're watching / They watch TV in the living room.' 

9 Helen is in her office. She's talking / She talks to somebody. 

10 What time are you usually having / do you usually have dinner? 

11 John isn't at home at the moment. He's visiting / He visits some friends. 

12 'Would you like some tea?' 'No, thank you. I'm not drinking / I don't drink tea.'

## 13 用动词的肯定式、否定式或疑问式填空。

## 现在时与过去时

Units 3-14 

## 15 用下列形式完成句子。

一般现在时 (I work/drive 等) 现在进行时 (I am working/driving 等)
一般过去时 (I worked/drove 等) 过去进行时 (I was working/driving 等)

1 You can turn off the television. I'm not watching (not/watch) it. 

2 Last night Jenny fell (fall) asleep while she was reading (read). 

3 Listen! Somebody ____ (play) the piano. 

4 'Have you got my key?' 'No, I ____ (give) it back to you.' 

5 David is very lazy. He ____ (not/like) hard work. 

6 Where ____ (your parents / go) for their holidays last year? 

7 I ____ (see) Diane yesterday. She ____ (drive) her new car. 

8 A: ____ (you/watch) television very much?
B: No, I haven't got a television set. 

9 A: What ____ (you/do) at 6 o'clock last Sunday morning?
B: I was in bed asleep. 

10 Andy isn't at home very much. He ____ (go) away a lot. 

11 I ____ (try) to find a job at the moment. It's very difficult. 

12 I'm tired this morning. I ____ (not/sleep) very well last night.

## 现在完成时（I have done 等）与一般过去时（I did 等）

Units 18–20 

## 19 用现在完成时或一般过去时的肯定式或否定式完成下列句子。

1 A: Do you like London?
B: I don't know. I haven't been there. 

2 A: Have you seen Kate?
B: Yes, I ____ saw ____ her five minutes ago. 

4 A: Are you tired this morning?
B: Yes, I ____ to bed late last night. 

5 A: Do you want this newspaper, or can I have it?
B: You can have it. I ____ it. 

6 A: Are you enjoying your new job?
B: I ____ yet. My first day is next Monday. 

7 A: The weather isn't very nice today, is it?
B: No, but it ____ nice yesterday. 

8 A: Was Helen at the party on Saturday?
B: I don't think so. I ____ her there. 

10 A: Is Silvia married?
B: Yes, she ____ married for five years. 

11 A: Have you heard of George Washington?
B: Of course. He ____ the first President of the United States. 

12 A: How long does it take to make a pizza?
B: I don't know. I ____ a pizza. 

## 20 用现在完成时或一般过去时造句。

1 A: Have you been to Thailand?
B: Yes, I went there last year. (I / go / there / last year) 

2 A: Do you like London?
B: I don't know. I've never been there. (I / never / there) 

3 A: What time is Paul going out?
B: ____ (he / already / go) 

4 A: Has Catherine gone home?
B: Yes, ____ (she / leave / at 4 o'clock) 

5 A: New York is my favourite city.
B: Is it? ____ ? (how many times / you / there?) 

6 A: What are you doing this weekend?
B: I don't know. (I / not / decide / yet) 

7 A: I can't find my address book. Have you seen it?
B: ____ (it / on the table / last night) 

8 A: Do you know the Japanese restaurant in Leeson Street?
B: Yes, (I / eat / there a few times) 

9 A: Paula and Sue are here.
B: Are they? ____ ? (what time / they / arrive?)

A: When the last time?
B: Two years ago.

## 23 选择正确答案。

1 'Is Sue working? (C)' 'No, she's on holiday.' A Does Sue work? B Is working Sue? C Is Sue working? D Does work Sue? 

2 'Where ____?' 'In a village near London.'
A lives your uncle B does your uncle live C your uncle lives
D does live your uncle 

3 I speak Italian, but ____ French.
A I speak not    B I'm not speaking    C I doesn't speak    D I don't speak 

4 'Where's Tom?' 'a shower at the moment.' A He's having B He have C He has D He has had

A were you    B was you    C you were    D have you been

A I'm seeing B I see C I was seeing D I've seen

A has Lisa phoned B Lisa has phoned C did Lisa phone D is Lisa phoning

A didn't see B don't see C hasn't seen D didn't saw

1 We were invited (invite) to the party, but we didn't go.
2 The museum is very popular. Every year it (visit) by thousands of people.
3 Many buildings (damage) in the storm last week.
4 A new road is going to (build) next year.
5 'Where's your jacket?' 'It (clean). It will be ready tomorrow.'
6 She's famous now, but in a few years her name will (forget).
7 'Shall I do the washing-up?' 'No, it (already/do).' 
8 Milk should (keep) in a fridge.
9 (you/ever/bite) by a snake?
10 My bag (steal) from my car yesterday afternoon.

8 When (the camera/invent)?

10 These shirts are clean now. I ____ (wash) them.

12 The information will ____ (send) to you as soon as possible.

## 32 选择正确答案。

1 Don't forget to switch (B) off the light before you go out.
A switch B to switch C switching 

2 It's late. I must ____ now.
A go B to go C going 

3 I'm sorry, but I haven't got time to you now.
A for talking B to talk C talking 

4 Gary is always in the kitchen. He enjoys A cook B to cook C cooking 

5 We've decided ____ away for a few days.
A go B to go C going 

6 You're making too much noise. Can you please stop A shout B to shout C shouting 

7 Would you like to dinner on Sunday?
A come B to come C coming 

8 That bag is too heavy for you. Let me .... you.
A help B to help C helping 

9 There's a swimming pool near my house. I go ____ every day.
A to swim B to swimming C swimming 

10 Did you use a dictionary ____ the letter?
A to translate B for translating C for translate 

11 I'd love ____ a car like yours.
A have B to have C having 

12 Could you me with this bag, please?
A help B to help C helping 

13 I don't mind ____ here, but I'd prefer to sit by the window.
A sit    B to sit    C sitting 

14 Do you want .... you?
A that I help    B me to help    C me helping 

15 I usually read the newspaper before ____ work.
A start B to start C starting 

16 I wasn't feeling very well, but the medicine made me ____ better.
A feel    B to feel    C feeling 

17 Shall I phone the restaurant ____ a table?
A for reserve    B for reserving    C to reserve 

18 Tom looked at me without ____ anything.
A say    B saying    C to say

## 学习指导

如果你不确定要学习哪些单元，可参考该学习指导。

从选项 (A、B、C 等) 中选择正确答案。有时答案不止一个。

如果你不知道或不确定正确答案是什么，请学习最右侧数字所对应的单元。在这些单元中可找到原句。该学习指导的答案请参见第314页。

## IF YOU ARE NOT SURE WHICH IS RIGHT

7.9 We ____ wait long for the bus – it came in a few minutes.
A don't have to B hadn't to C didn't have to D didn't had to E mustn't 

## IF YOU ARE NOT SURE WHICH IS RIGHT

A Are you liking B You like C Would you like D Do you like

A don't go B you no go C go not D you don't go

A working B works C worked D use to work E used to work

## 英语在用

剑桥“英语在用”（English in Use）丛书是一套享誉全球的英语学习用书，自出版以来，全球销量已逾千万册。丛书专为非英语国家的学习者编写，结构明晰，形式简约，重点突出，注重实用。鉴于剑桥“英语在用”丛书在学习者中的良好口碑，外语教学与研究出版社新引进了这套丛书的词汇、语法系列的修订新版，以及短语、习语等系列。希望读者朋友们通过这套高品质的学习用书，真正提高自己的英语水平。

《剑桥初级英语语法》是为初级学习者撰写的英语语法学习用书，简单易懂，既可用来自学，也可作为课堂教学辅助材料。

内容实用：取材于真实的语料库，涵盖基本语法结构及相关问题；

使用方便：每单元为一个对开页，左手页讲解语法，右手页编排相应练习，随学随练；

结构简明：分类解说语法点，方便师生挑选所需内容；

语法索引：将书中讲解的所有重要语法按字母顺序列出，并标注书中位置，方便查找；

补充练习：针对某些语法点进行重点练习加以巩固；

学习指导：测试语法知识，找出薄弱环节，并指出最适于学习的单元内容；

参考答案：详尽全面，便于学生自测学习效果，掌握进度。

## CAMBRIDGE INTERNATIONAL CORPUS

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a7d08640230795e3.jpg)


The Cambridge International Corpus (CIC) is a collection of over 1.5 billion words of real spoken and written English. The texts are stored in a database that can be searched to see how English is used. The CIC also includes the Cambridge Learner Corpus, a unique collection of over 35 million words taken from student exam papers from Cambridge ESOL. It shows real mistakes students make and highlights the parts of English which cause problems for students.
www.cambridge.org/corpus 

REAL ENGLISH GUARANTEE 

![image](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/beyondOurself/englishism/main/assets/egiu/a157fcafc0c4a01c.jpg)


此版本仅限在中华人民共和国境内（不包括香港特别行政区、澳门特别行政区及台湾省）销售。
